## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Kubernetes CRD Validation to OpenAPI Schema Publishing Chain

## Your Task

Trace how a CustomResourceDefinition's validation schema is converted to an OpenAPI schema in kubernetes/kubernetes. Find Go source files implementing: the CRD validation spec, the structural schema extraction, the OpenAPI v3 schema conversion, and the API server spec endpoint publication.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossrepo domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0, sg-evals/client-go--v0.32.0, sg-evals/api--v0.32.0, sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd.


## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{

  ],

  ],
  "chain": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "FunctionName"}
  ],
  "text": "Narrative explanation of your findings, citing repos and file paths."
}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

- **File recall and precision**: Did you find all relevant files?

## CRD Validation to OpenAPI Schema Publishing Chain

The chain spans the `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/` package in `sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0`:

### 1. CRD Validation Spec (Type Definitions)
- **`pkg/apis/apiextensions/types.go`** — Internal `CustomResourceValidation`, `CustomResourceDefinitionSpec`, `JSONSchemaProps`
- **`pkg/apis/apiextensions/v1/types.go`** — v1 API types with JSON tags
- **`pkg/apis/apiextensions/v1beta1/types.go`** — Legacy v1beta1 types

### 2. CRD Admission Validation
- **`pkg/apis/apiextensions/validation/validation.go`** — `ValidateCustomResourceDefinitionOpenAPISchema()` validates the schema at admission
- **`pkg/apis/apiextensions/validation/cel_validation.go`** — CEL validation context

### 3. Structural Schema Extraction
- **`pkg/apiserver/schema/structural.go`** — `Structural` type definition
- **`pkg/apiserver/schema/convert.go`** — `NewStructural()` converts `JSONSchemaProps` → `Structural`
- **`pkg/apiserver/schema/validation.go`** — `ValidateStructural()` checks structural invariants
- **`pkg/apiserver/schema/kubeopenapi.go`** — `ToKubeOpenAPI()` converts `Structural` → `spec.Schema`

### 4. OpenAPI Schema Conversion
- **`pkg/apiserver/validation/validation.go`** — `ConvertJSONSchemaPropsWithPostProcess()`, `NewSchemaValidator()`
- **`pkg/controller/openapi/v2/conversion.go`** — `ToStructuralOpenAPIV2()` strips v3-only fields
- **`pkg/controller/openapi/builder/builder.go`** — `generateBuilder()`, `buildKubeNative()`, `BuildOpenAPIV2()`, `BuildOpenAPIV3()`
- **`pkg/controller/openapi/builder/merge.go`** — `MergeSpecs()`, `MergeSpecsV3()`

It has the same field as admissionregistration.internal.WebhookClientConfig.\\n113: type WebhookClientConfig struct {\\n114: \\t// `url` gives the location of the webhook, in standard URL form\\n115: \\t// (`scheme://host:port/path`). Exactly one of `url` or `service`\\n116: \\t// must be specified.\\n117: \\t//\\n118: \\t// The `host` should not refer to a service running in the cluster; use\\n119: \\t// the `service` field instead.
